Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">aard</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nature, essence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a> (156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">altemaal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">altemȃle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all at once; altogether</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">allemal</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">all</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">everyone</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re doing it <b>all</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re <b>all</b> doing it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Despite its status as a pronoun, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a></i> can not serve as a subject in a sentence - in such cases it complements another pronoun. It can, however, serve as an object.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> (27)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***alstublieft.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a> (455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">belieft</i>, literally "if it pleases you". Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">s'il vous plaît</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> please</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> here you are (when handing something to someone else)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>Alstublieft</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally used when giving a payment to a salesperson, to which the salesperson responds with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> or an equivalent. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used by the salesperson when returning change to the customer, in which case the customer responds with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dank.html>dank</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> upon having received the change.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">a.<a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a>.b.</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i>Bijwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(formeel)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> beleefde aandrang <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> verzoek of versterking <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> bevel
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>Wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> doorlopen!</i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>Nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> witte paard ziek. <a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>Wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:alstublieft.html>alstublieft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> drank <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:volgende.html>Volgende</a> week <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> Holland <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> paard <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> daken rijden.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Het_hele_jaar_rond:_van_Sinterklaas_tot_Sintemaarten,_p._13_3-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Het_hele_jaar_rond:_van_Sinterklaas_tot_Sintemaarten,_p._13-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>'</dd></dl></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">altijt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> tijt</i> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">altijts</i>), equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***ander.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> (495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">andar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*anþeraz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">other</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a></b> zijde.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>other</b> side.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">different</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a></b> fiets, <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fijn.html>fijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I want a <b>different</b> bike, I don't sit well on this one.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">second</span></li></ol>

</p>

***avond.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a> (510)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">âvont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">āvont</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ēbanþs</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avonden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>evening, night</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Just like German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Abend</i>, Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:avond.html>avond</a></i> includes the hours until midnight. So while one says in English: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'re having a beer tonight!</i>, one would say in Dutch: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vanavond.html>vanavond</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> biertje!</i>
</p>

***bang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a> (240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">banghe</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">be-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">anghe</i>, the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an adverbial form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">enge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow, confined</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">angst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>banger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bangst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scared, frightened
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>Wees</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Please don't be <b>afraid</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> donker!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I am <b>scared</b> of the dark!</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>fearful</li>
<li>anxious</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> accompanied with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i> (to be); for example: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></i> "I am afraid". Usage with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> (to have) also occurs - for example: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></i> - but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> generally proscribed.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bevreesd</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">angstig</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vruchtig</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">verschrikt</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bangen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sound of an explosion or gun; <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a></a></li></ol>
<hr />

***bed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> (414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bedde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bedde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*badją</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bedden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bedje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">furniture for sleeping</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">garden<span class="ib-comma">,</span> agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">patch</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">layer</span>, often a substratum</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> of a body of water
<ul><li><b>1950</b>, Willy <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> der Heide, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>Drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> onbewoond eiland</i>, Stenvert.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>gegeven</a> ogenblik stieten <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> uitgedroogde beekbedding; <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> beek <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> naakte lava.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> instituut <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> capaciteit <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 100 <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bedden</a></b></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a> (431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bel.html>bel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ring, like using a bell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, by bell (originally) or (now mostly) telephone; to dial</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">afbellen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">opbellen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bellan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bellaną</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bellow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:bellen.html>bellen</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">блеять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blejatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baa, bleat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_dialects" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch dialects">Southern</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bark, like a canine</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> (29)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a></i>, as an imperative, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered non-standard, the standard form being <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>Created in analogy to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">am</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*betst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*batistaz</i>, superlative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gōdaz</i>. ***bezig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a> (482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bēsich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bisig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bisīg</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>beziger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bezigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>busy, occupied
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He can not talk right now. He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>busy</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> (69)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>at, with
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>Bij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> feest.</i>
<dl><dd><b>With</b> us it's always a party.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>by, close to
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> woon in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> hutje <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zee.</i>
<dl><dd>I live in a little hut <b>by</b> the sea.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to, towards
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>Kom</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a>!</i>
<dl><dd>Come to <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> by, through, by means of, through the action or presence of</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bië</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bīa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bijō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bee, insect of the clade Anthophila</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a> (367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>With regular loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">blijde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">blide</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*blīthi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blīþiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blijer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">blijst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">happy</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> straten wit <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If the streets are white, the children are <b>happy</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">glad</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">blijdschap</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bli</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lead (metal)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">blee</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Blei</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blij.html>blijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lead (metal)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the colour of lead</li></ol>

***blijven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a> (226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bliven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">blīvan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bilībaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stay, to remain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:blijf.html>Blijf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Stay</b> here, I'm going to have a look.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stay, to remain, to still be</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep/keep on, to continue to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeurt.html>gebeurt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:blijven.html>blijven</a></b> lachen!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Whatever happens, always <b>keep</b> laughing!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***bloed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloed.html>bloed</a> (502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bloet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bluot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*blōþą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:bloed.html>bloed</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">blood</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Blut</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">blod</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bloed.html>bloed</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>blood
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:bloed.html>Bloed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rood.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Blood</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> red.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a grave consequence, a high price</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a whole body; especially <i>(plural also (archaic) <b>bloeien</b> in this sense)</i> a (poor) person</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a> (1312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bôom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bōm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baumaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>bomen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tree</li>
<li>any solid, pole-shaped, usually wooden object
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">beam</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mast</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">mast</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">giek</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">be</i>+ <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">oven</i>.
Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">bufan</i>.
</p><p>See also Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">ovan</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bringan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bringaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰrenk-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring, to carry</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deliver, to supply</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a> (299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">buten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*būtan</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">but</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">baussen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">bûten</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">buute</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-nl">buten</i>.

***daar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> (67)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dâer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>there</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">ginds</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ginder</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>See Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_2">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>since (preceding a reason why something <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> like it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> zin <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Since she doesn't feel like it, she won't come</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aangezien</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>omdat</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voegwoord"><i>Voegwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:geeft.html>geeft</a> <b>onderschikkend</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> reden <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> ziek <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vergadering <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> voorzitten.</i> </li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vergadering <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> voorzitten <b><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> ziek <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> ruzie, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> gezellig.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> verschillende <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaatsen</a>
<dl><dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> opgevallen <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> hotel <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></b> sporen vertoont <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> achterstallig onderhoud. <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> eenmaal <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoveel.html>zoveel</a> gasten <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vroeg.html>vroeger</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>Ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>daaraan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meneer.html>meneer</a> Wang <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> streeft <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>volle</a> bezetting.</i><sup id="cite_ref-Grand_Hotel_Europa,_p._16_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Grand_Hotel_Europa,_p._16-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarom.html>daarom</a> (347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">daeromme</i>. <li>therefore, so, that's why</li>
<li>thereby, because of that
<dl><dd><i>Polymethylmethacrylaat <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a> ongeveer 90% <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> licht <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:daarom.html>daarom</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruiken.html>gebruikt</a> ter vervanging <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> glas, ten opzichte <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> aantal voordelen biedt: <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> lichter, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> versplintert <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> eenvoudig in allerlei vormen <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> produceren, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> licht <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a> glas.</i>  |  PMMA lets through approximately 90% of light and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thereby often used as a substitute for glass, with respect to which it offers a number of advantages: it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> lighter, it does not break in shards, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> simpler to produce into all kinds of forms, it lets through more light than normal glass.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***dag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> (149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dagaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">daagje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>day <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">period of 24 hours</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>daytime <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">time between sunrise and sunset</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In archaic or dialectal usage, the older plural form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>daag</a></i> may occur after numerals. On rare occasions the expression <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">veertien <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>daag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fortnight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still found in contemporary standard Dutch.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_3">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_10">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>daggen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A piece of rope, used to punish sailors with, on the spot or in running the gauntlet</li>
<li>A line used to fasten young sailors while training boarding a hostile ship or climbing the rigging</li></ol>

***dagen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a> (356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dāgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dagon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dagāną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dawn</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to light, illuminate, color by lighting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, begin</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to become understood</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subpoena, summon to appear in court</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to call, summon to battle, notably against uproar</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> (38)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>then, at that time <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the future</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>Morgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beter.html>beter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Tomorrow the weather will be better, but then I must go to work again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>then, after that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>Eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> tanden poetsen, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">First you need to brush your teeth, then you may go to <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>then, in that case
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> geregend of gesneeuwd <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> veilig <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> not rained or snowed, then the car must still be safe.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The adverb <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> almost obligatorily used in Dutch after an imperative with a preceding conditional clause:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a>, bezoekt <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a></b> in ieder geval <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> haven.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If you have the time, then be sure to visit the harbour.</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>

***dat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> (6)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">that</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þat</i>, neuter form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sa</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">das</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">that</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>that (neuter); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person further away.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>that</b> house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>that</b> child</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><br />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">datzelfde</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">demonstrative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that, that there
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>that</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> demonstrative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> clipping of <b><span class="Latn" lang="nl">datzelfde</span></b></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that same (thig), the aforementioned
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">–Voordat <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> weggaat, <a href = vnd.unilang:zet.html>zet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> afval <a href = vnd.unilang:buiten.html>buiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a>!<br />–Okee, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>).</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">–Before you leave, take the rubbish out please!<br />–Okay, I will do <b>that</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> who, which, that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I know a girl <b>who</b> can do that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">exophoric</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that, those (regardless of gender and number)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>That</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Those</b> are men.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p><p>A preceding comma may alter the meaning of a clause starting with a relative pronoun. Compare the following sentences:
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> boek <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> wit <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I returned the book <b>that</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> white. (The white book specifically, not another)</span></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> boek, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></b> wit <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terug.html>terug</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I returned the book, <b>which</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> white. (The book happened to be white)</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_3">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>that

<p>An unstressed variety of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>. </p>
<ol><li>the <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">definite article, masculine and feminine singular, plural</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> (masculine singular)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The woman (feminine singular)</span></div></dd>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_3">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Placed before masculine and feminine nouns in the singular and plural nouns of all genders, indicating a specific person or thing instead of a general case.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ul><li>There <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also the clitic form <i>'s</i> for <i>des</i>. The oblique cases are archaic and found in contemporary Dutch only in fixed idiomatic phrases (e.g., <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> den duur</i>).</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thenken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*þankijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þankijaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*teng-</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dōre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">duere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">duri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*durz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰwer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">doorway, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>, gate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***dicht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a> (506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thīht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þinhtaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tight</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dichter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">dichtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thick, tight, dense</li>
<li>close
<dl><dd><i>„Wie vorig <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> woning verkocht, <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>kreeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> prijs <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> relatief <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> oorspronkelijke vraagprijs lag”, <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> onderzoek.</i> — “Who in the previous year sold his home, obtained a price that lay relatively <b>close</b> to the original asking price,” stated the research paper. <br /><small>(<i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ad.nl/economie/article962441.ece"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Algemeen Dagblad</a></i>, 5 January 2007)</small></dd></dl></li>
<li>closed, shut
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> spring lachend in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> diepe <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> m'n <a href = vnd.unilang:ogen.html>ogen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a></b>.</i> — I jump laughing into the deep with my eyes <i>shut</i>. <small> (Marco Borsato ft. Sita  |  <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>Lopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> Water) </small></dd></dl></li></ol>
