***die.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> (23)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i>, a merger of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thē</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thia</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thiu</i> and similar forms of the demonstrative. As in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ther</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">der</i> it replaced the original masculine and feminine nominative forms from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>that (masculine, feminine); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to a thing or a person further away.</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>that</b> tree</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a></i>
<dl><dd><b>that</b> woman</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>those (plural); <span class="use-with-mention">referring to things or people further away.</span>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> vensters</i>
<dl><dd><b>those</b> windows</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>


<p><br />
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> who, whom, which, that
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I don't know any people <b>who</b> can do that.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a>!</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, but I know somebody <b>who</b> can!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_4">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>A preceding comma may alter the meaning of a clause starting with a relative pronoun. Compare the following sentences:
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a> arbeiders <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> staken <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> sancties <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> rekenen.</i>
<dl><dd>All workers <b>who</b> are on strike should expect sanctions.</dd></dl></li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a> arbeiders, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></b> staken, <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> sancties <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> rekenen.</i>
<dl><dd>All workers, <b>who</b> are on strike, should expect sanctions.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<p>In the first sentence, only the workers on strike are advised to expect sanctions. In the second sentence, the parenthetical phrase indicates that all the workers are on strike, and should all expect sanctions.
</p>

***dingen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a> (229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to convene, to plead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thingon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þingōną</i>. The verb <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally weak, but became strong by analogy with other verbs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dingen.html>dingen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to solicit</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a> (445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dôden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*dōden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daudijaną</i>. Compare English <i>deaden</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Gij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zult.html>zult</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:doden.html>doden</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Thou shalt not <b>kill</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***doen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a> (63)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">duon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰéh₁t</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> in.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Just <b>put</b> it in there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to, to make; <span class="use-with-mention">forms causative verbs</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> vorig <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <b>makes</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> think of last year; i.e. that reminds <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> of last year.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a></i> + indefinite pronoun, sometimes with postpositioned <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be different; to make a difference
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> beide camera's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:elkaar.html>elkaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a>).</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The two cameras <b>are</b>n’t much <b>different</b> [i.e. neither <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> much better than the other].</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with an adjective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to behave or act in some way
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>Doe</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Just <b>act</b> normal.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used as the finite verb after the fronting of an infinitive.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>Werken</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She didn't work anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***dus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> (101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">dos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>thus, so, ergo</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Voegwoord"><i>Voegwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> reden, <a href = vnd.unilang:daarom.html>daarom</a> (signaalwoord)
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a> warm <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a></b> trek <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> trui <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>.</i> </li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ēhaft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwahaftaz</i>.

***een.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> (9)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">êen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ein</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*óynos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></strong> (<i>contracted form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">'n</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Placed before a singular noun, indicating a general case of a person or thing:</span> a, an. Compare with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>one</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">aaneen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bijeen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">eenheid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">eenmaal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">eenzaam</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">enig</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iedereen.html>iedereen</a></span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>When it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear from the context whether <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the number or the indefinite article, the former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written with acute accents: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">één</i>. In all other cases it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written without. For example, <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 'one of those'. But <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> appel</i> can mean both 'one apple' and 'an apple', so if the former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> intended one would write <i><b>één</b> appel</i>.</li></ul>
<dl><dt>Examples</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a></b> hoed</i>: a hat; <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> oor</i>; an ear.</li>
<li><i><b>Eén</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> allen, allen <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b>één</b></i>: one for all, all for one. (The motto of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Three_Musketeers" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Three Musketeers">The Three Musketeers</a>.)</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Lidwoord"><i>Lidwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> meervouden in uitroepende zinnen <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> verbazing <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> aantal uitdrukken

***eerder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a> (494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Reformed by epenthesis of <i>-d-</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eerre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ēriro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*airizô</i>, an adjective formed from the comparative adverb <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*airiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>earlier, former
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerdere</a></b> stijl <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leuk.html>leuker</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His <b>former</b> style <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> funnier.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vroeg.html>vroeger</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>previous, prior
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerdere</a></b> voorstellen <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> ambitieuzer.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">His <b>initial</b> proposals were more ambitious.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eerder.html>eerder</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>earlier

***en.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> (10)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_4">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ende</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ande</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">inde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*andi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂entí</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_3">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>and
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> zee.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Old_Man_and_the_Sea" class="extiw" title="w:en:The Old Man and the Sea">The Old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a> <b>and</b> the Sea.</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>well, so
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>ermee</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Well</b>, how're you doing?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a></b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Well</b>?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>So</b> what?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plus, and
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>Drie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> zeven.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Three <b>plus</b> four <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seven.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_4">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ne</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ne</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></span> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> not
<ul><li>"Herr Halewyn", A.H. Hoffmann von Fallersleben, <i>Horae Belgicae</i>, page 41.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">‘<a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>Uw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> heer Halewyn <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> gaen jagen, / g’ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziet.html>ziet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> weêr <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>levens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a>.’</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">'Your son Lord Halewyn has gone hunting / you <b>won't</b> see him again for the rest of your life.'</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">...<a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> aldaer <a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a> Utrecht <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> geacht ende respecteert <b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a>, ...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that in Utrecht <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no longer valued and respected...</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">masculine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> feminine<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <b><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i></b></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> only one
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> bezwaar <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>You are the <b>only one</b> who has objections.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neuter<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <b><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i></b></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> only thing
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>bomen</a>.</i>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The superlative form <b>enigste</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> commonly used, but people may see it as wrong. The form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></i> correct, but the use of it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> discouraged. See <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://taaladvies.net/taal/advies/vraag/262/">http://taaladvies.<a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a>/taal/advies/<a href = vnd.unilang:vraag.html>vraag</a>/262/</a> (in Dutch) for more information.
</p>

***er.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> (18)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Weak form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">der</i>, the unstressed form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i> ("there")
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>there <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unspecific to distance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> him, her, it, them.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>ermee</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>gewerkt</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I have worked <b>with it/them</b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> bergen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>You can see the mountains <b>above it/them</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an unstressed variety of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i>, used when it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not needed to emphasize the specific location relative to the speaker.</li>
<li>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iro</i>, genitive of the personal pronoun (3rd person plural).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">partitive pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> of them, of those (often not translated in English)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>My brother has three children and I have two. (<i>literally:</i> two of those)</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I don't see any more (of them).</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i>Bijwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ergent</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ergen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">irgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iergin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iowergin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*euhwargin</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hwergin</i> (gt; Middle Low German <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">ergent</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hwergin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">iowergin</i> (gt; Middle High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">iergen</i>, gt; German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">irgend</i>), Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hwerġen</i>, Old Norse <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hvargi</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> (259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ēten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">etan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*etaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁édti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a></strong>

***even.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> (103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">effen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*evan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ebnaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>shortly, briefly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I shall have a look for you <b>shortly</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for a short period, for a while
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> tweede helft <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> 19e eeuw bloeide Vollenhove <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>.<sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/VollenhoveGeschiedenis">[3]</a></sup></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the second half of the 19th century, Vollenhove flourished again <b>for a while</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>; <span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating that the speaker expects that something will require little time or effort.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>Zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deur.html>deur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dicht.html>dicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Could you please close the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> (<b>for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a></b>)?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>just as, to the same degree <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">used with an adjective</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> midden <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vloer <a href = vnd.unilang:staan.html>stond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> tafel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> meter hoog <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> stoel <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the middle of the floor there stood a four-metre tall table and a chair <b>just as</b> large beside it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quite, rather
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a></b> kwaad!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He's <b>rather</b> angry!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
